               </a>
              </h3>
             </header>
             <p class="dek">
              Certain blocks of Main Street from Commerce to Rusk, will now be closed off to drivers, so businesses can expand their outside patio seating into the roadway.Its part of the city of Houston's pilot program called More Space: Main Street, which aims at helping restaurants and bars downtown recover from the pandemic.
             </p>
             <!-- -->
             <!-- -->
            </div>
           </article>

            <div class="info">
             <header class="info-header">
              <h3 class="title">
               <a href="/news/little-dipper-bar-becomes-first-downtown-business-to-expand-patio-seating-onto-roadway-part-of-city-program">
                Little Dipper Bar becomes first downtown business to expand patio seating onto roadway, part of city program
               </a>
              </h3>
             </header>
             <p class="dek">
              Certain blocks of Main Street from Commerce to Rusk, will now be closed off to drivers, so businesses can expand their outside patio seating into the roadway.Its part of the city of Houston's pilot program called More Space: Main Street, which aims at helping restaurants and bars downtown recover from the pandemic.
             </p>

              <h3 class="title">
               <a href="/whats-your-point/voter-integrity-or-suppression-depends-on-what-side-your-on-whats-your-point">
                Voter integrity or suppression, depends on what side your on - What's Your Point
               </a>
              </h3>
             </header>
             <p class="dek">
              During the pandemic, Harris County tried a lot of different ways to get voters to vote and the numbers at the poll indicate it was a success, but there are concerns about hacking and possible fraud. New legislation in the Texas Senate hopes to settle it once and for all.
